[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run of the Mongoose JSON parsing code triggered an [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer-detected stack-buffer-overflow in the function `mg_json_get` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlocated in `src/mongoose/src/json.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The overflow is a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write past the end[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof a local buffer named `nesting`, and it occurs during fuzz testing via the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness in `test/fuzz.c`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzzing with libFuzzer, an AddressSanitizer error was reported:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  * A stack-buffer-overflow of one byte in `mg_json_get` at line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m of `json.c`.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  * The write overruns the local array `nesting`, which is declared at line [0m[1;36m131[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhas a length of [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  * The overflow happens when `mg_json_get` is invoked by the fuzzing entrypoint [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `test/fuzz.c`.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a stack-based buffer overflow: a write beyond the bounds of a fixed-size [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal array on the stack.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The sanitizer trace pinpoints the overflow to `mg_json_get` in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/mongoose/src/json.[0m[1;92mc:186:28[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The local variable `nesting` in that function is too small for certain inputs,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to a write at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwell beyond its [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m-byte size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mongoose/test/fuzz.c`, around line [0m[1;36m81[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply calls [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get` on arbitrary input, and so is triggering the bug without additional [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic interference.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The stack frame dump and shadow-byte legend confirm this is not a false [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpositive: the redzones around the buffer are violated by a single-byte write.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas to investigate for a holistic view  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The implementation of `mg_json_get` in **src/mongoose/src/json.c**, in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparticular:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – The declaration and sizing of the `nesting` array [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m131[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Any loops or indexing logic that write into `nesting`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Related helper functions in the same file, e.g., path processing routines.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzing harness in **mongoose/test/fuzz.c**, specifically the call on line [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m, to understand how inputs are fed into `mg_json_get`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any JSON path or nesting–level handling code in the JSON module that may [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfluence index calculations or buffer management.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
